      <script type="text/javascript">
       var destinations = [{name:'afrique',id:'1',countries:[{name:'burkina faso',id:'10'},{name:'namibie',id:'11'}]}];
 var months = {"Janvier":1,"Février":2,"Mars":3,"Avril":4,"Mai":5,"Juin":6,"Juillet":7,"Août":8,"Septembre":9,"Octobre":10,"Novembre":11,"Décembre":12};
 var now = new Date();
 var dateNames = ["Janvier "+now.getFullYear(), "Février "+now.getFullYear(), "Mars "+now.getFullYear(), "Avril "+now.getFullYear(), "Mai "+now.getFullYear(), "Juin "+now.getFullYear(),"Juillet "+now.getFullYear(), "Août "+now.getFullYear(), "Septembre "+now.getFullYear(), "Octobre "+now.getFullYear(), "Novembre "+now.getFullYear(), "Décembre "+now.getFullYear(),"Janvier "+(now.getFullYear()+1), "Février "+(now.getFullYear()+1), "Mars "+(now.getFullYear()+1), "Avril "+(now.getFullYear()+1), "Mai "+(now.getFullYear()+1), "Juin "+(now.getFullYear()+1),"Juillet "+(now.getFullYear()+1), "Août "+(now.getFullYear()+1), "Septembre "+(now.getFullYear()+1), "Octobre "+(now.getFullYear()+1), "Novembre "+(now.getFullYear()+1), "Décembre "+(now.getFullYear()+1)];
 var dates = [{month:dateNames[now.getMonth()]},{month:dateNames[now.getMonth()+1]},{month:dateNames[now.getMonth()+2]},{month:dateNames[now.getMonth()+3]},{month:dateNames[now.getMonth()+4]},{month:dateNames[now.getMonth()+5]},{month:dateNames[now.getMonth()+6]},{month:dateNames[now.getMonth()+7]},{month:dateNames[now.getMonth()+8]},{month:dateNames[now.getMonth()+9]},{month:dateNames[now.getMonth()+10]},{month:dateNames[now.getMonth()+11]}];
 var durations = [{duration:'1'},{duration:'2'},{duration:'3'},{duration:'4'},{duration:'5'},{duration:'6'},{duration:'7'},{duration:'8'},{duration:'10'},{duration:'11'},{duration:'12'},{duration:'13'},{duration:'14'},{duration:'15'},{duration:'16'},{duration:'17'},{duration:'18'},{duration:'19'},{duration:'20'},{duration:'21'},{duration:'28'}];
 
 function InterfaceViewModel(destinations,dates,durations) {
     var self = this;
     self.destination = ko.observable(false);
     self.date = ko.observable(false);
     self.duration = ko.observable(false);
     self.destinations = ko.observableArray(destinations);
     self.dates = ko.observableArray(dates);
     self.durations = ko.observableArray(durations);
     self.displayDestination = function(item) {
 	    self.destination(item);
     }
   	self.displayDate = function(item) {
 	    self.date(item);
     }
     self.displayDuration = function(item) {
 	    self.duration(item);
     }
     self.removeDestination = function(item) {
     	self.destination(item).remove;
     	self.destination(false);
     }
     self.removeDate = function(item) {
     	self.date(item).remove;
     	self.date(false);
     }
     self.removeDuration = function(item) {
     	self.duration(item).remove;
     	self.duration(false);
     }
 	self.values = ko.computed(function() {
 		// toJS pour créer un tableau
 		// getJSON pour get url...
 		var values = ko.toJSON({
 			destination: self.destination != false ? self.destination().id : false
 		});
 		return values;
 	});
 }
 ko.applyBindings(new InterfaceViewModel(destinations,dates,durations));
      </script>
      <script type="text/javascript">
       $(document).ready(function () {
 	function activateSubmenuFilters(row) {
 		var $row = $(row),
 			submenuId = $row.data("submenufiltersId"),
 			$submenu = $("#" + submenuId),
 			height = $menu.outerHeight(),
 			width = $menu.outerWidth();
 		$submenu.css({display: "block"});
 		$row.find("a").addClass("maintainHover");
 	}
 
 	function deactivateSubmenuFilters(row) {
 		var $row = $(row),
 		submenuId = $row.data("submenufiltersId"),
 		$submenu = $("#" + submenuId);
 		$submenu.css("display", "none");
 		$row.find("a").removeClass("maintainHover");
 	}
 
 	$(".DropdownMenu.filters").menuAim({
 		activate: activateSubmenuFilters,
 		deactivate: deactivateSubmenuFilters
 	});
 
 	$(".DropdownMenu.filters li").each(function() {
 	  	var total = $(this).find('span.total').text();
 	  	var region = $(this).find('span.region').text();
 	  	var url = $(this).find('.DropdownMenu-a').attr('href');
 		var maplabel = '#'+region.toString();
 		if (maplabel != '#') {
 			$("div[id=" + region + "]").find('.MapLabel-total').text(total + ' départs');
 			$("div[id=" + region + "]").find('a').attr('href',url);
 		}
 	});
 
 	$("a.duration").on('click touchstart', function() {
   		var max = $(this).find("span").text();
   		window.location = ('/recherche-voyages/1?f[duration][]='+max);
 	});
 
 	$("a.depart").on('click touchstart', function() {
 		var periode = $(this).find("span").text();  		
   		var year = periode.substr(-4);
   		var month = periode.substring(0,periode.indexOf(" ",0));
   		var monthnumber = months[month];
   		if(monthnumber < 10) {monthnumber = '0'+monthnumber;}
   		window.location = ('/recherche-voyages/1?f[month_start][]='+year+'-'+monthnumber);
 	});
 	
 	$('.Map-l path').addClass('darkmap');
 	var alldropdown = $('.DropdownMenu.filters');
 	var allfilters = $('.Map-optionlink');
 	var allarrowsright = $('.icon-right-arrow');
 	var allarrowsleft = $('.icon-left-arrow');	
 	var btnclose = $('.CloseFilters');
 	btnclose.click(function(e){
 		allarrowsleft.addClass('mask');
 		allarrowsright.removeClass('mask');
 		allfilters.removeClass('open').next().css('display','none');
 		$(this).css('display','none');
 	});
 	$('.Map-optionlink').click(function(e) {
 		e.preventDefault();
 		allarrowsleft.addClass('mask');
 		allarrowsright.removeClass('mask');
 		btnclose.css('display','block');
 		btnclose.css('cursor','pointer');
 		var left = $(this).find('.icon-left-arrow');
 		var right = $(this).find('.icon-right-arrow');
 		if($(this).text() == 'Destinations') {btnclose.css('right','10px');} else {btnclose.css('right','53%');}
 		if($(this).hasClass('open')) {
 			if(left.hasClass('mask')) {right.removeClass('mask');}
 			$(this).removeClass('open');
 			$(this).next().css('display','none');
 		} else {
 			if(left.hasClass('mask')) {left.removeClass('mask');right.addClass('mask');} 
 			allfilters.removeClass('open');
 			allfilters.next().css('display','none');
 			$(this).addClass('open');
 			$(this).next().css('display','block');
 		}
 	});
 });
      </script>
     </section>

   <script type="text/javascript">
    var $menu = $(".DropdownMenu.search");
 	function activateSubmenu(row) {
 		var $row = $(row),
 			submenuId = $row.data("submenuId"),
 			$submenu = $("#" + submenuId),
 			height = $menu.outerHeight(),
 			width = $menu.outerWidth();
 		$submenu.css({
 			display: "block"
 		});
 		$row.find("a").addClass("maintainHover");
 		var mapID = $submenu.parent().find('.DropdownMenu-a').attr('id');
 		$('.Map-s path').removeClass('showmap').addClass('initmap');
 		$menu.find('path#'+mapID).removeClass('initmap');
 		$menu.find('path#'+mapID).addClass('showmap');
 		$('.Map-resultfix').css('display', 'none');
 		$submenu.parent().find('.Map-resultfix').css('display', 'block');
 	}
 	function deactivateSubmenu(row) {
 		var $row = $(row),
 		submenuId = $row.data("submenuId"),
 		$submenu = $("#" + submenuId);
 		$submenu.css("display", "none");
 		$row.find("a").removeClass("maintainHover");
 	}
 	$(".DropdownMenu.search").menuAim({
 		activate: activateSubmenu,
 		deactivate: deactivateSubmenu
 	});
 
 "use strict";
 $(document).ready(function () {
 
 	if (jQuery.isMobile()) {
 		$("meta[name=viewport]").attr('content','');
 	}
 	$('#affix').fixTo('.Main', { useNativeSticky:false });
 	$('.Map-s path').addClass('initmap');
 	// initialize the megamenu
 	$('.MenuSearch-filters').accessibleMegaMenu({
 		/* prefix for generated unique id attributes, which are required
 		   to indicate aria-owns, aria-controls and aria-labelledby */
 		uuidPrefix: "accessible-megamenu",
 		/* css class used to define the megamenu styling */
 		menuClass: "nav",
 		/* css class for a top-level navigation item in the megamenu */
 		topNavItemClass: "MenuSearch-item",
 		/* css class for a megamenu panel */
 		panelClass: "DropdownMenu",
 		/* css class for a group of items within a megamenu panel */
 		panelGroupClass: "DropdownPopover",
 		/* css class for the hover state */
 		hoverClass: "hover",
 		/* css class for the focus state */
 		focusClass: "focus",
 		/* css class for the open state */
 		openClass: "open"
 	});
 
 	// hack so that the megamenu doesn't show flash of css animation after the page loads.
 	setTimeout(function () {
 		$('body').removeClass('init');
 	}, 500);
 
 	$(".scroll").click(function(e){		
 		e.preventDefault();
 		$('html,body').animate({scrollTop:$('[id="'+this.hash.substring(1)+'"]').offset().top}, 500);
 	});
 
 		$('.Account-signin-link').iform({
 		href: '/iform/usersignin/user/signin/?r=L3VzZXIvYWNjb3VudA%253D%253D'
 	});
 	$('.Account-wishlist-link').iform({
 		href: '/iform/usersignin/user/signin/?r=L3VzZXIvYWNjb3VudC93aXNobGlzdC8%253D'
 	});
 	});
 $(window).scroll(function() {
 	if ($(this).scrollTop()>0) {$('.TopPage').fadeIn();} else {$('.TopPage').fadeOut();}
  });
   </script>
  </body>
 </html>
